Islamic Republic of Pakistan Bilawal Bhutto Zardari at UN Headquarters." srcSet="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/240/cpsprodpb/1997/production/_129515560_gettyimages-1248012702-594x594.jpg 240w, ee0ct7c0"/></picture></span><span role="text" class="ssrcss-tvuve5-StyledFigureCopyright e34k3c20"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e1y6uwnp0">Image source, </span>Getty Images</span></div><figcaption class="ssrcss-1mget3o-StyledFigureCaption e34k3c22"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e1y6uwnp0">Image caption, </span><div spacing="6" class="ssrcss-y7krbn-Stack e1y4nx260">Bilawal Bhutto Zardari will be the first Pakistani foreign minister to visit India since 2011</div></figcaption></figure></div><div data-component="byline-block" class="ssrcss-1bdte2-BylineComponentWrapper e8mq1e90"><div class="ssrcss-qt5zqv-BylineWrapper e8mq1e917"><div class="ssrcss-19r1h8t-ContributorContainer e8mq1e916"><div class="ssrcss-1bsxjdu-Container-ContributorPhoto e8mq1e912"><div class="ssrcss-1f4spe2-ImageWrapper e8mq1e911"><span class="ssrcss-pfpsqa-Placeholder e16icw910"><span><noscript><img alt="Soutik Biswas" src="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/80/cpsprodpb/0129/production/_112979200_soutikbiswas.jpg" width="80" height="80" loading="lazy" class="ssrcss-evoj7m-Image ee0ct7c0"/></noscript></span></span></div></div><div class="ssrcss-1qc7pto-Container-ContributorDetails e8mq1e913"><div class="ssrcss-68pt20-Text-TextContributorName e8mq1e96"><div class="ssrcss-1q14p6q-LinkWithChevronContainer e8mq1e91"><a href="https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/correspondents/soutikbiswas" class="ssrcss-lo1ylm-StyledLink e8mq1e92">By Soutik Biswas</a><span class="ssrcss-o1g7k8-IconContainer-IconContainerChevron e8mq1e93"><svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" width="1em" height="1em" class="ssrcss-xi5oyi-StyledIcon e6m7o991" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M21.6 14.3 5.5 31h6.4l14.6-15L11.9 1H5.5l16.1 16.7v-3.4z"></path></svg></span></div></div><div class="ssrcss-84ltp5-Text e8mq1e910">India correspondent</div></div></div></div><div class="ssrcss-jlwt2c-Divider e8mq1e915"></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00"><b class="ssrcss-hmf8ql-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Bilawal Bhutto Zardari is in Goa to participate in a conference of the Shanghai Cooperation Organisation - the first Pakistani foreign minister to visit India since 2011.</b></p></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">Hina Rabbani Khar met her Indian counterpart SM Krishna in Delhi <a href="https://www.bbc.com/news/world-south-asia-14291484" class="ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0">12 years ago</a>, but circumstances were different then. India and Pakistan were experiencing a limited thaw, and trying to boost trade. Pakistan&#x27;s relationship with the US was in a crisis. &quot;The diplomatic moment back then was ripe for attempts at rapprochement. It&#x27;s a different story today,&quot; Michael Kugelman of The Wilson Centre, an American think-tank, says.</p></div></div><div data-component="unordered-list-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-1o5f7ft-BulletListContainer e5tfeyi0"><ul role="list"><li><a href="https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-india-64396138" class="ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0">India and Pakistan came close to nuclear war: Pompeo</a></li></ul></div></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">The countries have fought three wars since they became independent nations in 1947. All but one were over Kashmir. In 2019, <a href="https://www.reuters.com/graphics/INDIA-KASHMIR/010090XM162/index.html" class="ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0">India launched strikes in Pakistani territory</a> following a <a href="https://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-india-47302467" class="ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0">militant attack on Indian troops</a> in Kashmir. After the attacks, the two countries had come &quot;close&quot; to a nuclear war, former US Secretary of State Mike Pompeo claimed in his recent memoir.</p></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">But a new border truce concluded in 2021 has kept things under control. When India accidentally fired a supersonic missile into Pakistan last year, Islamabad issued a statement condemning the launch, without escalating the incident into a serious crisis. &quot;But this isn&#x27;t to say the relationship is in a safe place. It&#x27;s always on tenterhooks, even at the best of times,&quot; says Mr Kugelman. &quot;Today, it would only take one trigger, one provocation, to take the two sides back up the escalatory ladder.&quot;</p></div></div><div data-component="image-block" class="ssrcss-xza2yt-ComponentWrapper ep2nwvo1"><figure class="ssrcss-wpgbih-StyledFigure e34k3c23"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-11kpz0x-Placeholder e16icw910"><span><noscript><picture><source srcSet="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/240/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg.webp 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/320/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg.webp 320w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/480/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg.webp 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/624/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg.webp 624w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/800/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg.webp 800w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/976/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg.webp 976w" type="image/webp"/><img alt="An Indian Army Soldier looks through a 84 MM RL Gun at a Forward Post at LoC Line Of Control in Uri, Baramulla, Jammu and Kashmir, India on 02 April 2022. T" srcSet="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/240/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/320/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg 320w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/480/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/624/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg 624w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/800/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg 800w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/976/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg 976w" src="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/976/cpsprodpb/10FAF/production/_129515596_gettyimages-1239697500-594x594.jpg" width="976" height="549" loading="lazy" class="ssrcss-evoj7m-Image ee0ct7c0"/></picture></noscript></span></span><span role="text" class="ssrcss-tvuve5-StyledFigureCopyright e34k3c20"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e1y6uwnp0">Image source, </span>Getty Images</span></div><figcaption class="ssrcss-1mget3o-StyledFigureCaption e34k3c22"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e1y6uwnp0">Image caption, </span><div spacing="6" class="ssrcss-y7krbn-Stack e1y4nx260">An Indian soldier on the de-facto India-Pakistan border - a 2021 truce has kept things under control</div></figcaption></figure></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">Not surprisingly, expectations from Mr Bhutto Zardari&#x27;s visit to the popular beach destination of Goa are low. Before landing in India, he said his visit was &quot;focussed exclusively on the SCO&quot; and that he looked forward to &quot;constructive discussions with my counterparts from friendly countries&quot;. </p></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">Mr Bhutto Zardari&#x27;s  visit underlines, &quot;most of all that both India and Pakistan attach great significance to the interface with the Shanghai Cooperation Council (SCO),&quot; says TCA Raghavan, a former Indian high commissioner to Pakistan. </p></div></div><div id="piano-inline1"></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">The SCO, founded in 2001 to discuss security and economic matters in Central Asia, is led by China, a key Pakistani ally, and Russia, an important emerging friend of Pakistan. It also includes four members from Central Asia, a region that Islamabad hopes to engage more for trade, connectivity and energy. &quot;For Islamabad skipping the conference would raise the risk of Pakistan being isolated from an organisation that embraces its interests strongly,&quot; says Mr Kugelman. </p></div></div><div data-component="unordered-list-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-1o5f7ft-BulletListContainer e5tfeyi0"><ul role="list"><li><a href="https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-india-47382949" class="ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0">India and Pakistan in &#x27;uncharted waters&#x27;</a></li></ul></div></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">No bilateral meetings are expected to take place between Mr Bhutto Zardari and his Indian counterpart S Jaishankar. &quot;Apart from the fact that a Pakistani foreign minister has not visited India in a long time, this visit is pretty much inconsequential in the larger bilateral context,&quot; Happymon Jacob of Jawaharlal Nehru University in Delhi, says.  </p></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">Husain Haqqani, a former Pakistani ambassador to America who is now at the Hudson Institute in Washington, DC, echoes a similar sentiment: &quot;The visit, per se, does not represent any thaw in the relationship.&quot; </p></div></div><div data-component="image-block" class="ssrcss-xza2yt-ComponentWrapper ep2nwvo1"><figure class="ssrcss-wpgbih-StyledFigure e34k3c23"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-11kpz0x-Placeholder e16icw910"><span><noscript><picture><source srcSet="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/240/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg.webp 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/320/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg.webp 320w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/480/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg.webp 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/624/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg.webp 624w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/800/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg.webp 800w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/976/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg.webp 976w" type="image/webp"/><img alt="Pakistan Foreign minister Hina Rabbani Khar and External affair minister S.M. Krishna meet at the Hyderabad house in New Delhi. 2011" srcSet="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/240/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/320/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg 320w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/480/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/624/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg 624w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/800/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg 800w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/976/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg 976w" src="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/976/cpsprodpb/B168/production/_129561454_gettyimages-119920620-594x594.jpg" width="976" height="549" loading="lazy" class="ssrcss-evoj7m-Image ee0ct7c0"/></picture></noscript></span></span><span role="text" class="ssrcss-tvuve5-StyledFigureCopyright e34k3c20"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e1y6uwnp0">Image source, </span>Getty Images</span></div><figcaption class="ssrcss-1mget3o-StyledFigureCaption e34k3c22"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e1y6uwnp0">Image caption, </span><div spacing="6" class="ssrcss-y7krbn-Stack e1y4nx260">Hina Rabbani Khar met her Indian counterpart SM Krishna in Delhi in 2011</div></figcaption></figure></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">It&#x27;s best to look at the Pakistani foreign minister&#x27;s visit through a &quot;multilateral lens, not a bilateral one,&quot; says Mr Kugelman. &quot;He&#x27;s not going to pursue reconciliation with Delhi. He&#x27;s going to participate in a conference of regional organisation that holds considerable importance for Pakistan&#x27;s interests.&quot;</p></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">That leaves the two rivals frozen in what Prof Jacob describes as &quot;cold peace&quot;. He says: &quot;Neither side wants to rock the boat but has no appetite to make significant concessions to seek or begin a dialogue on the outstanding issues.&quot; Mr Raghavan believes the &quot;relationship has been stable for the past two years or so but at a low plateau&quot;. Mr Haqqani likens the relationship to &quot;being on a treadmill with periodic ups and downs&quot;.</p></div></div><div data-component="unordered-list-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-1o5f7ft-BulletListContainer e5tfeyi0"><ul role="list"><li><a href="https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-india-49737886" class="ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0">How to read Indian threat to Pakistan over Kashmir</a></li></ul></div></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">The redeeming reality is that both countries have a strong interest in keeping tensions down. &quot;Pakistan is facing an internal mess and can&#x27;t afford a fresh crisis with India. And India is increasingly concerned about China, its biggest security challenge, and doesn&#x27;t want to have additional trouble on its western front from Pakistan,&quot; says Mr Kugelman.</p></div></div><div id="piano-inline2"></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">But if both sides have an interest in reducing tensions, why isn&#x27;t the summit in India an opportunity to pursue long-lasting reconciliation? Clearly, politics stands in the way. </p></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-11r1m41-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00">&quot;There would be considerable public backlash in either country if efforts are made to pursue peace. This would be especially costly in Pakistan, where the government is already deeply unpopular and in over its head,&quot; says Mr Kugelman.  </p></div></div><div data-component="image-block"
